Can Lifebuoys Really Save the Poor? 137

"Break Glass in Emergency"

Xu Fuming Distorts Meaning Due to Desperation

Breaks Glass Hoping Someone Will Come to Help

Xu Fuming, a 36-year-old native of Jiaxing, has been unemployed for a long time. He is now extremely poor and despondent, spending his days in idle chatter. The other day, at dusk around 5:30 PM, he went alone to the Bund and wandered back and forth along the Huangpu River. He then went to a pier, where he saw a glass cabinet containing a lifebuoy. Suddenly, he smashed the glass with his palm. Just as he was about to take the lifebuoy, he was discovered by a patrolman, who arrested him for damaging public property without cause and took him to the Old Zhabei Police Station. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the First Special District Local Court. The police lawyer, Ru Baoyi, filed a complaint against him for damage under Article 198 of the Criminal Code, requesting that he be punished. Judge Feng Shide asked him why he damaged the property, and his answer was so ridiculous and unexpected that it elicited laughter. He claimed that he had been unemployed for a long time and his life was extremely difficult. Yesterday, he happened to be walking to the pier and saw the words "Break this glass in an emergency." Since he had no means of making a living and was in dire straits, he broke the glass, thinking that if he obtained the lifebuoy, someone would come to his rescue. Those who heard this could not help but smile. Judge Feng explained that the lifebuoy was for rescuing those drowning in the Huangpu River and that "emergency" referred to rescuing the drowning. The defendant misunderstood the meaning of the words and violated the criminal law. He was leniently sentenced to ten days of detention, suspended for two years. After the sentence, he was dismissed. It was indeed an amusing incident.

Over 43,000 Taels, and a record of a sum of over 43,000 Taels received by the Wanfeng Company, the numbers are the same, and the receipt and payment are on the same day. Based on this, if the defendant did not falsely use the name of Yan Deji and privately used the company's silver of over 43,000 Taels, then the defendant privately paid Yan Deji the debt owed to the Wanfeng Company and transferred it to the company. In reality, over 43,000 Taels were taken from the company to pay off his privately owned Wanfeng Company. His breach of trust and benefiting himself at the expense of the company is clear. Moreover, Yan Deji declared at the last board meeting that he had no dealings with the company, which further proves that the money was indeed used by the defendant to cheat and enrich himself, and he is suspected of violating Article 366 of the Criminal Code. (2) The defendant recommended Jin Youyun as the company's accountant, with a monthly salary of 80 yuan. However, Jin spent over 15,900 taels last year. In fact, over 13,000 taels were transferred from the Wanfeng Company, a situation similar to the Yan Deji incident mentioned above. This situation is a deliberate damage of the company's property and is suspected of violating Article 366 of the Criminal Code. (3) The defendant is responsible for the issuance and safekeeping of stocks. There are many unissued stocks. The defendant claimed that it was for the convenience of issuance and asked the directors to sign and stamp in advance. Once these unissued stocks are filled in with the amount of capital, they are no different from formal stocks and are equivalent to cash. However, 19 of them have disappeared without a trace, only empty. He lived peacefully in Ruifengsha. Unexpectedly, his helmsman waited for his master on the boat, and when he did not return in the evening, he began to search for him the next morning. He searched for several days along the downstream coastal areas, Chuansha Bailonggang, Gaoqiao Donghaitang, etc. Since he had no trace of his master and did not see the small sampan his master was driving, he was very anxious and had no choice but to report to his son. After hearing the news, his son reported it to the ship management office of the customs, notifying the affiliated offices to pay attention to the investigation. He also went to various relatives and friends to investigate, and the news of his disappearance spread throughout Shanghai. A few days ago, he personally went to Wusong several times to search, but returned without any results. It was not until the 2nd of this month that a shamin came to Wusong to report that he knew for sure, so he went to pick him up by sailing boat, and arrived safely in Shanghai that night. According to his own account, when the small sampan he was riding in was chased by a raging tide, he recruited a sand boat to tow it back to Song. Later, seeing that the boat was heading towards the outer sea, he was afraid that there was something wrong, so he cut the tow rope and let it drift in the Yangtze River Estuary, hoping that a steamship or sailing boat would pass by so that he could ask for help. Unexpectedly, it was drifted by the tide to Ruifengsha and he had to live in the home of a villager and ask someone to send a letter to Wusong.

Fuzhou Dehe Company's Accountant

Jiang Xiuzhen Appropriated the Goods' Funds for Himself 138

丨Has Been Arrested Awaiting Document for Transfer丨

Jiang Xiuzhen, a 29-year-old Fujian native, served as an accountant at the Dehe Grocery Company in Fuzhou. The owner of the company, which has been in operation for many years with thriving business, is Hong Baoming, also a Fujian native. Last month, Hong handed over 9,305 yuan, 1 jiao, and 3 fen in paper money that he had collected to Jiang, entrusting him to purchase a gasoline ship and 1,600 yuan worth of white sugar from the local customs. However, after receiving the large sum, Jiang had malicious intentions. He did not purchase the goods as agreed but privately deposited the funds in the local Central Bank, transferring them to the Central Bank of Shanghai for storage and opening an account in his own name. Jiang also abandoned his job and fled to Shanghai, lodging in Room 8 of the Jiangsu Hotel on Zhejiang Road. Hong Baoming learned of this and reported it to the Fuzhou Provincial Public Security Bureau, which sent a document to the Shanghai Public Security Bureau and the Songhu Garrison Headquarters requesting assistance in the investigation. At the same time, he notified the Central Bank of Fuzhou and sent a telegram to the Shanghai branch to stop payment. On the first of this month, Jiang Xiuzhen, due to the inability to withdraw funds from the Central Bank, hired Lawyer Yang to go to the Old Zhabei Police Station to ask for help. The head of the police station believed that this was a civil matter and refused to handle it. The other day, the Old Zhabei Police Station suddenly received a document from the Songhu Garrison Headquarters stating the matter of Jiang Xiuzhen's embezzlement of a large sum of money. Therefore, they sent Chinese detective Wang Ruilin to bring Jiang into the police station, and notified the garrison department. Yesterday morning, they were transferred to the Summary Court of the First Special District Court. The garrison department sent Inspector Xu Pengfei with instructions to the case, stating that this case was telegraphed by the Fuzhou Public Security Bureau to the ministry for assistance, so please allow the transfer so that it can be transferred to Fuzhou. However, the official document has not yet been prepared due to the time constraint, and it will be supplemented later. Then, the lawyer hired by Hong Baoming rose to state the above situation, saying that all the funds were successively paid by the Dehe Company to the Fuzhou Nanfu Qianzhuang, entrusting Jiang to purchase steamships and white sugar, with Nanfu receipts as proof. Police lawyer Qian Xunjiu said that the police station's role in this case is also to assist. Now that the plaintiff and the garrison department have submitted considerable evidence, the police station does not oppose the transfer of this case. Moreover, Jiang Xiuzhen is not a resident of the concession, please verify. When asked of Jiang, he also hired two lawyers to go to court to argue against the transfer and apply for bail. Judge Liu Yugui verified the confession and ordered that the case be verified again after the official document from the garrison headquarters arrives. Jiang Xiuzhen was allowed to be released on bail of 5,000 yuan pending further instructions.

Husband Becoming More Depraved Daily

Wife Also Unable To Endure Poverty 139

Neighbors Repeatedly Tempted Her

Leading To Her Being Sold Into Prostitution

Sun Baichuan, a Nanjing native residing at No. 4 Yongshun Lane, Tangjia Bay, Nanshi, has become more depraved and does not engage in proper work in recent years. His wife, Gao, is only 19 years old and has a particularly beautiful appearance. She often feels like a phoenix following a crow. In addition, her husband does not seek self-reliance, and life has become increasingly uncomfortable, leading her to become more resentful and self-pitying. Gai Dingcheng, a neighbor, often visits the Sun family. Although he recognizes Gao, he initially did not inquire about her due to the suspicion of impropriety. Recently, he has discerned the lady's hidden feelings. Whenever there is no one around, he advances with seductive words, saying that staying with this poor fool will never bring happiness. If she can abandon him and leave, she will have plenty of food and clothing and endless enjoyment. The lady initially remained unmoved. After Gai seduced her again and again, she finally fled with Gai on the 14th of last month and was taken into the brothel established by the Yangzhou woman Wang Chen at No. 3 Yongan Lane, Guangxi Road. From then on, she became a prostitute, available for anyone to pluck. Although Sun Baichuan has lost his beloved wife, he does not care. However, his father-in-law, Feng, has lost his treasured daughter and has been searching for her all day. The detective immediately took the suspect to the Zhabei Police Station and dispatched investigator Yang Dechun to arrest Wang Chen and Sun Gao, who claimed to be prostitutes, having already received more than ten customers and having been renamed Aizhen by the madam. Yesterday morning, they were all taken to the First Special District Local Court. Judge Feng Shide examined them. After the police lawyer, Ru Baoyi, explained the case, Detective Liu requested that all the defendants in the case be transferred. Judge Feng asked Wang Chen and others about the case, and then approved the transfer to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for investigation.

French Concession Police Solve

Morphine Factory Case Interrogation Concluded 140

German Continues to Evade Responsibility

Thorough Investigation Leads to Clarification

On January 12 of this year, the Municipal Public Security Bureau dispatched a police brigade together with the second precinct of the sixth district and solved a large-scale morphine manufacturing factory in the French Concession, detaining the German Bate, Chinese Tong Rongbao, Jin A'gen, and others. They confiscated a large box of morphine and raw materials, as well as machinery and other items. The factory houses were sealed and all the defendants were transferred to the local court, where the prosecutor investigated and prosecuted them. Yesterday morning, the judge Guan opened the court. According to Bate's confession, he is American, and Klein is the factory owner. He signed a contract with him as an engineer. It is a factory that makes perfume. I don't know about morphine. I only went to work for three days and was arrested. There were only three workers, and the factory had not been established or opened yet. As for the box of nicotine, it was discovered after I went there. When I asked the factory owner, he said that it was also used for making morphine medicine, so I told him to take it away, otherwise I would not do it, but it was not taken away, and I was arrested. Tong Rongbao confessed that he is a native of Ningbo and was introduced by his younger brother to a Frenchman to work as a worker on the 7th. His job was to sweep the floor and wipe the windows. Their sign was Shanghai Perfume Company. We only saw Bate. We sometimes supplied him with water, but after going to work, we did not get paid. Jin A'gen confessed that he is a native of Zhenjiang. He went to the perfume company as a shop assistant, introduced by a foreigner. He worked for a total of four days. As for the foreign boss, he only saw Bate, who could say a few words of Chinese to direct us. There was also a worker named Su Ruigen. The factory building has more than ten rooms in three courtyards, and the machines are in the third courtyard. We didn't see how Bate was making it, and he didn't need us. According to Inspector Zhang Cunde, there was also perfume in the factory, but not much. The materials for making morphine were found in Bate's box. At this point, the case became clear, and Prosecutor Zhang was asked to come to court to state his opinion. After the defendant's lawyer made a defense, the judge ordered the end of the defense and waited for the sentence.

Shuttle Alley

Robbery and Shooting in Early Morning 141

Pregnant Woman and Child Also Grazed by Bullets

The morning of yesterday, at approximately 9:00 AM, in the Shuttle Alley, No. 12 Dengyun Bridge, in the city, Mrs. Shi, residing in the upstairs room of the厢房, left her home carrying her child to go shopping. Regrettably, before she exited the alleyway, two bandits approached her, intercepted her path, and forcibly seized one of the gold bracelets from her wrist. Additionally, the child's foot was also grazed by the bullet. Subsequently, upon receiving news of the incident, the police station of the second district dispatched officers to the scene. However, the two bandits had already made their escape, leaving no trace. The injured woman was transported to the hospital for medical treatment by police vehicle.

A Rotten Male Corpse in the Huangpu River 142

Around noon yesterday, a dredging boat from the Junpu Bureau was dredging mud in the Huangpu River outside Lujiazui in Pudong. Suddenly, the mud bucket dredged up the body of a man. The body was already rotten and the face was blurred and unrecognizable. The clothes, socks, and shoes he was wearing were also difficult to distinguish. It was estimated that the body had been submerged in the river for several months. It was difficult to determine whether he had been murdered and his body deliberately sunk to the bottom of the river to prevent it from resurfacing. The crew of the boat stopped the machine and moved the body aside. They then reported to the Customs Water Police Station, which dispatched a sampan to drag the body back to the river surface near the police station. The Life Saving Bureau patrol boat was notified to report to the court to determine the cause of death, and then arrangements would be made for burial. An investigation will be made to see if anyone claims the body.

Settlement of Rent Dispute in Xichongye Lane 146

The rent dispute in Xichongye Lane on East and West North Sichuan Road has been entangled in litigation for half a year and is difficult to resolve. Now, the owner, Mr. Chen Xiaodie, entrusted lawyer Wu Zhiping to directly negotiate with lawyer Lu Qi, the representative of the Tenants' Association. Only then did he understand the details and express his concession. In consideration of the difficulties faced by businesses, he generously agreed to special sacrifices. It is said that the conditions have been negotiated properly, namely, all tenants in West Xichongye Lane are exempted from rent for five months, and the rent is reduced by one month per year. Counting from January 28 to the end of July, a total of six months of rent will be exempted. On the date of signing the agreement, half of all the arrears will be paid in advance at lawyer Lu Qi's office, and the remaining arrears will be paid monthly with the new rent for one month. The deadline for clearing the payment is the end of April. The lawsuits will be withdrawn by each party, and the costs will be borne by each party. As for the tenants who have paid the rent in advance, they can still exchange the previously received rent receipts for the new rent receipts issued this time at lawyer Lu Qi's office, so as to ensure uniformity and complete the procedures. The storm has ended, and both parties are very satisfied.

Supplementary Teaching Materials for the January 28th Incident 148

▲The Municipal Education Bureau Orders Schools to Adopt Them

The Municipal Education Bureau has issued a special order to all municipal primary schools regarding the issue of using the special edition for the January 28th Commemoration Day as supplementary teaching materials for primary schools: "The January 28th Incident last year was an important commemoration day for this city, and it is an excellent opportunity to promote patriotic education. However, this year's commemoration day falls during the winter vacation of various schools in the city. In order to commemorate the January 28th Incident, all schools should, during the first week of the next semester, list the January 28th Incident as the central issue of teaching, and strive to arouse the spirit of nationalism. In addition, the bureau has entrusted the Morning Post to compile and publish a special edition for the January 28th Commemoration Day. The content includes patriotic teaching materials for low, medium, and high grade levels. All schools should uniformly adopt it as supplementary teaching materials for primary schools. For this purpose, all schools are hereby notified to purchase and distribute the materials from the bureau within three days of receiving this document, according to the number of children in each school. Spring and Autumn

Lady Vanity 164

— Zhan Lu

The unbreakable Lunar New Year sees many fashionable men and women showing off their new clothes everywhere. Does the impending national crisis diminish their interest? I gleefully overheard a very harsh "Lady Vanity" jest in the background, which I will write down later as a timely warning for illiterate women who love vanity!

Lady Vanity opened her gilded box and was lost in thought!

She has a genuine fur coat and a soft satin skirt, but unfortunately, a brand-new overcoat covers them, preventing people from appreciating her beauty within. Yet, if she doesn't wear the overcoat, how can she compete with other ladies in overcoats to see who is the most stylish?

She came up with a hilariously bizarre plan! She begged someone to write two notes, one reading "Genuine fur coat inside" to hang on her chest, and the other "Soft satin skirt inside" to hang on her abdomen. This way, her beautiful clothes inside the overcoat wouldn't be completely hidden.

She walked among the crowds, indeed attracting a lot of attention. She proudly believed that her plan was brilliant. However, due to the jostling in the busy market, after walking for a while, the signs on her chest and abdomen were squeezed off!

Lady Vanity, having lost her signs, could no longer flaunt her beauty within! She was frustrated, but then she smiled again. Why? Because she picked up two notes by the roadside. Being illiterate, she assumed they were what she had lost and re-attached them, one above and one below.

She walked into the busy market again, oh no! Disaster struck! The traffic was blocked! She was surrounded by a sea of people! She panicked and desperately called for help. Fortunately, the police were able to rescue her from the siege, immediately tearing off the signs and questioning why she was wearing these attention-grabbing notes. Lady Vanity, somewhat regaining her composure, reported the whole story to the police.

"Madam, you can't even read, yet you want to show off? The one you wore on your chest was a note that fell off someone's door: 'Honored guests, please ring the bell here.' The one you wore on your abdomen was a note that fell off the toilet: 'Gentlemen, please step closer when urinating.'"

My Family's Old Gatekeeper 165

— Juan Yun

My family's old gatekeeper is named Zhang, and he is over sixty years old. He served on the battlefield for more than twenty years. His hometown is in Hunan. He joined the Xiang Army at the age of nineteen and rose through the ranks to become a squad leader, with the qualifications of a company commander. He is honest and forthright, so we call him Old Zhang.

In recent years, seeing the rampant Japanese pirates and the precarious state of the nation, he often sighed and occasionally talked to me about his anti-Japanese war in the Jiawu Year (1894).

He remembered that it was the nineteenth year of the Guangxu Emperor's reign. Li Hongzhang was demoted to Governor-General of Liangguang, and Grand Scholar Wang Wenshao was in power. Urgent pleas from Korea arrived like snowflakes. Wang Wenshao advocated for war, so Wu Dacheng, the Governor of Hunan at the time, volunteered to be the vanguard, leading two hundred battalions of the Xiang Army, marching heroically out of Shanhaiguan. Old Zhang was a squad leader in the Fifth Battalion under Wu Dacheng's command, wearing a victory jacket and a martial arts headscarf, leading over a hundred infantrymen.

At that time, the Jingfeng Railway only extended to Shanhaiguan, and it was their first time using trains.

Li Guangjiu, the general guarding Shanhaiguan, was the bravest and most skilled, leading eleven battalions of the old Xiang Army. In addition, there were sixty battalions of Li Hongzhang's Huai Army, totaling more than 150,000 soldiers, including troops from various places.

Newly arriving at the front lines, their courage was tenfold. They won two major battles in a row. The Japanese pirates were pushed back to the vicinity of Haicheng. Once past Haicheng, it would be Korean territory. If they pursued their victory, it would not be difficult to defeat the Japanese pirates completely. At the same time, Liu Yongfu was also gaining ground in Fujian. Unexpectedly, Li Hongzhang secretly sabotaged the effort, strongly advocating for peace, willing to cede land and pay reparations, and secretly intercepting ammunition. His intentions were incompatible with Wang Wenshao, and he wanted to see all the advocates for war suffer a crushing defeat! He was so insane that the fate of China was left in the hands of one person!

Naturally, if Japan had been defeated at that time, it would not have been so rampant today.

Silvery West Lake 166

— Recorded and Photographed by Zhou Yunting

Standing in Lakeside Park, looking up at the snow after the rain on West Lake, the white expanse of the lake is shrouded in ice and snow. The towering peaks in front are all silvery, like wearing pure white robes. Moreover, people exploring the plum blossoms on Gushan Island are gathering courage, walking in groups in the snow.

Novel

Taking a Photo 167

— Mo Yi

"Is this your residence?" The man looked at Zhang Rongjiu and said, "I am extremely tired from walking and would like to have some water. Please give me... Oh... Ouch..."

Zhang Rongjiu listened without saying anything, just nodded and went into the house to fetch water.

After Zhang Rongjiu went into the house, the man turned around, smiled at Zhao Tian, and said enthusiastically:

"If we join the Volunteer Army like them, we will definitely wipe out those wicked enemies! Like those three you just mentioned... What's wrong? Those three...?"

"That's right! We must fight to the death... Those three? Well, this is what happened: yesterday morning, three members of the Volunteer Army, carrying broadswords, looking just like Huang Tianba on stage, came here to scout the road. We told them everything in detail. Good lads, they really are something! That night, we heard gunfire all night..."

At this moment, Zhang Rongjiu came out of the house with a bowl of water. Hearing Zhao Da's careless words, he shouted loudly:

"Old Zhao, why do you talk so much nonsense? Did you see those three members of the Volunteer Army with your own eyes? You didn't sleep last night and are talking in your sleep this morning!" Zhang Rongjiu handed the bowl of water to the man and added, "Don't listen to him, Old Zhao is famous for boasting around here; he's just joking with you because you mentioned the Volunteer Army!"

A patch of dark clouds was blown over from the northwest corner by a howling gale. In an instant, the sun, which had struggled to emerge, succumbed again to the cloud cover, which resembled a smoke screen. The man slowly drank the water, his eyes darting across the faces of the three, a smug smile on his face.

××××

On September 16th, as the people of Chestnut Gully Village were eating lunch, goose-palm-sized snowflakes were rolled into clumps by the roaring northwest wind, landing with such force that they were almost like bombs dropped from a bomber, capable of killing a person. At this time, apart from three groups of yellow figures wriggling in the snow, nothing else could be seen. (3)

Listening to his words, I strongly recalled the anti-Japanese war of the 19th Route Army, so I closed my eyes and said nothing.

Cohabitation ABCs 168

— Bai He

One cannot always embrace bachelorhood. As a dignified man, one cannot remain unmarried forever. Having a wife means maintaining a family and fulfilling the obligations of marital cohabitation. However, how to enjoy family life through marital cohabitation is a significant question. Now, I will share my wifely arts for readers who have wives but do not enjoy family life for careful discussion.

There is a saying: "Love your wife, respect your mother-in-law." To please your wife, you must treat your mother-in-law with the reverence of the Jade Emperor, without any disobedience. Her food, clothing, and housing are naturally indispensable, and you must not object to her drinking or smoking opium. Because of loving your wife and respecting your mother-in-law, you must extend your affection to her father, brother-in-law, sister-in-law, and other relatives. You must take care of them attentively. When your in-laws pass away, you must, without saying, mourn and conduct the funeral with propriety, making the later funeral even grander than the previous one. Even when your brother-in-law marries or your sister-in-law gets married, you must be generous with all the arrangements, even if it means going into debt.

As a husband, the money earned through hard work outside should be given entirely to your wife. This is a natural obligation. Even the deeds, IOUs, and accumulated savings from childhood must be handed over to your wife for safekeeping and management. A husband must not be selfish. If a husband needs to stay out late or has any extramarital ambitions, he must seek his wife's opinion beforehand. Because the husband is the wife's husband, he should not disregard her opinions.

Thirdly, the wife's life should be entirely according to her preferences. For example, if the wife enjoys socializing with male friends, the husband should not interfere. If the wife wants to listen to operas and eat gourmet food every night, the husband should not frown at her. If the wife likes to sleep until three in the afternoon every day, the husband is not allowed to make loud noises and disturb her good sleep. These are just a few examples. In short, the wife's life should be allowed to develop naturally as a matter of course.

On Ornaments 169

— Guo Lanxin

Among objects, there are practical ones and there are ornaments.

Looking at people, there is also a distinction between practical and ornamental. Among the masses, some are able to establish a career, seeking happiness for the entire human race, the entire world, and the entire nation. Others seek benefits for society and the local community, thus living up to being a useful person. Yet, some are idle all day long, lacking purpose, ability, and soul. They are nothing more than walking corpses, ornaments among the crowd. Ornaments among objects only occupy space, but they can enhance the aesthetics and artistry of the arrangement. Ornaments among people are completely useless and consume useful resources instead. A group of these ornaments gathered together can lead society down a path of stagnation and decline, being harmful and not beneficial. Ah, these superfluous ornaments.

In these times of national crisis, as citizens who live off the land, we should all rise up to fulfill our national responsibilities, taking on the task of breaking through the national crisis. Walking corpses and ornaments should be overthrown and eliminated. Ah, this group of superfluous ornamental people will gather in those decadent, degenerate, and romantic places to indulge in pleasure during this period of intense national crisis, as if heeding their burial knell.

Shanghai Night Talk 170

— Zhang Ruogu

New Hawaii

On New Year's Eve, I planned to go to the Shanghai City God Temple with my partner, Comrade Huang, to visit Murocha. Murocha is an art scholar who praises the Temple as a cultural center. We wanted to invite him to join us, believing it would add a lot of interest.

In a square-tiled living room, two red candles burned brightly on an Eight Immortals table, with offerings of pastries and candies to the ancestors in the middle. Murocha was talking with two young ladies wearing black overcoats in the 1934 Russian-style. They were both genuine young ladies from the city and classmates of Murocha's sister. We were all acquaintances, so we joined the conversation without restraint. Carried away by the scene, we unconsciously drifted away from the idea of going to the City God Temple's all-night bazaar and the burning of the first incense.

Just as we were about to bring up the idea of going to the City God Temple, Murocha immediately said, "I am not against participating in this kind of public event, but I am afraid of being surrounded by beggars. If you are interested in joining the excitement, it is better to go together when it is dawn."

We were indifferent and did not necessarily have to rush to the night market. Finally, we changed our plans at the last minute. The five of us strolled along Xiafei Road from the West Gate, which was as bright as day.

At midnight, we were already sitting around a small table at the "New Hawaii" midnight dance hall at the intersection of Luban Road.

Outside, the wind was strong, and a tall black doorman in a thick overcoat stood guard behind the door. Inside, it was a different world. The fire in the stove was burning very warmly, and the entire place was decorated in a tropical style, almost making us forget that it was winter.

The ceiling was an artificial blue sky, which gave an even fresher feeling than the ceiling decoration of "Black Eyes." Three large lanterns with colorful patterns cast a faint light, as if we were in a magnificent Eastern palace. The four walls were painted in light green and blue, with several slanted palm trees and broad-leaved banana trees. Four colorful glass mirrors depicted four naked men and women. One was Eve, our first mother, in the Garden of Eden, holding an apple in her hand, leaning against a tree branch, her eyes filled with alluring expressions. Behind us was Josephine Baker, the famous Parisian dancer, completely naked, with a string of bananas hanging around her waist, dancing a Hula. To the right of the music stand was a picture of natives of Honolulu playing music, wearing white clothes and trousers, with garlands around their necks, playing the ukulele. A dozen or so small square tables were covered with white cloths, on which were coral-colored vases and ashtrays, and daffodils sent out a burst of fragrance. Several musicians on stage were playing popular jazz tunes.

The two young ladies from the city were surprised to see the banana dance image hanging behind them as soon as they sat down, and they said in unison:

"Such a painting is truly hideous and indecent."

Murocha replied, "Look at the slender palm trees, the broad-leaved banana trees, the brown-skinned woman, how healthy her body is! She is barefoot, dancing in the desert, how carefree and natural! This is a common sight in tropical regions. I think it is painted very well, there is nothing indecent about it!"

A White Russian waiter came to greet us, and we ordered three glasses of vodka, two cups of coffee, and a bottle of Shanghai beer.

The soul-stirring music, the sensuous portraits, the heat from the stove, and the stimulating power of the coffee finally aroused the interest of the men and women. Couples danced gracefully on the smooth floor. Murocha, who hadn't danced for six or seven years, and Comrade Huang, who hadn't set foot in a dance hall for more than a year, also accompanied the two young ladies in waltzes and foxtrots.

They danced until after two o'clock in the morning, still with great interest. I sat alone at the table, smoked five "My Love" cigarettes, drank two glasses of Shanghai beer, and listened to the conversation of three Germans and two Frenchmen at the next table. They were all in high spirits and seemed to be discussing some secret matter.

Because the two young ladies had to rush to their relatives' home in the City God Temple to eat wontons and dumplings, we left the heated "New Hawaii" before three o'clock at dawn. In the freezing wind, the three men and two women shivered and went their separate ways.

Qian Zhuang to Open Account Books Today 176

Shanghai's Qian Zhuang, following customary procedures, begins sending account books and opening accounts at the start of each lunar new year. Now that the Lantern Festival is approaching, it is customary to open and distribute account books, so the Qian Zhuang have mostly decided to start sending account books today (the 4th), distributing them in succession until the Lantern Festival, when all will be delivered. Therefore, Qian Zhuang employees have been very busy on the road recently.

Yarn and Cotton

Weakness in Foreign Cotton, Sluggish Sales, Relaxation of Standard Yarn 178

The yarn market has turned weak again, with a particularly weak upward momentum. This is due to the sluggishness of foreign markets, which has dampened sentiment, and the instability of the domestic situation, with tensions escalating in North China. As for the interior, commercial decline is dire, making it difficult to revive yarn sales. However, some are still strongly considering price increases due to the low base price. Based on the overall situation, there is a risk of further decline.

(Public Bidding: Flat Morning, Low Afternoon) In the previous market, the opening price for public bidding was flat due to the weakness of foreign cotton, but the residual momentum from the previous day had not subsided, and the market remained strong. Far-month contracts rose by 12 qian. In the afternoon, it was heard that actual demand had cooled, and raw cotton also fell, with each month falling by 3, 4, 5, and 6 qian. Disappointment Among Bulls, Closing Positions in Standard Cotton 179

The cotton market has started to decline again, and the strong momentum from the previous day has completely dissipated. This is because the Indian and American cotton markets remain weak. Indian cotton trading houses are still hawking cotton in the market and are very willing to make price concessions in order to find a way out, as the market is flooded with new cotton and sales are lacking, leading to increased hedging. As a result, the market has plummeted. As for American cotton, overproduction and sluggish consumption have also led to price instability. The Cotton Appraisal Committee on February 1st made no changes to the standards, which remain the same as in the previous period.

(This Month's Cotton Falls by 4 Qian) In the previous market, the opening price for Zheng Biao cotton was weak. Most people had expected American cotton to rise, but the telegraphic report was flat, greatly disappointing the bulls. The market suddenly fell, with each month falling by 1.5 to 2.5 qian. In the afternoon, bulls closed positions, making the market even weaker, with each month falling by 1 to 2 qian. The total volume of transactions for the day was 44,100 dan. Sales included 7,500 dan of Jifeng, 2,300 dan of Tonghe, 2,300 dan of Xincheng, 1,300 dan of Chunjie, and 1,600 dan of Yuchang. Grains: Rice Market Sluggish, Sales Stagnant, Another 4 Jiao Drop 182

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, there were over 30 sources, but sales were sluggish, with only over 1,000 shi traded. As a result, the market fell again, with prices following suit. Su Tong varieties fell by about 4 jiao. Qingjiao varieties were revised down by 2 to 3 jiao. The early market for Nangang Hou Shao rice was slightly soft, but the market continued to fall by 4 jiao. Duyang Jian and Yinyuan were scarce, creating a tight situation, and market prices were able to hold steady. For factory rice, only Yangjian was priced at 9 yuan. Chang varieties saw no market.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, 14 or 15 boats arrived from downriver. Baijing rice had sluggish sales because customers had profits to gain and wanted to sell quickly. In addition, scattered囤戶(speculators) successively sold, leading to sluggish sales and a market decline of 3 to 4 jiao. Slightly more Bo Dao rice arrived, with some retail sales possible at a small discount. Early rice arrivals continued, with more sluggish sales at a small discount of 3 jiao. Not many Yang Du Jian arrived, with sales still possible at a small discount of 1 to 2 jiao. Kejian saw a small discount of 1 to 2 jiao for Yinyuan.

Both Guest Xian and Local Xian Active 183

▲Market Temporarily Stabilizing

Yesterday, both guest Xian and local Xian rice had active demand, allowing the market to stabilize. There is hope for further development in the local market because the river's尖米(high-quality rice) is currently scarce and expensive, and its quality is not as good as客秈 (Xian rice for guests or people from out of town) hence it is welcomed by consumers, and there are also囤戶 (speculators) who seize the opportunity to buy small quantities, making the outlook very good. However, the market's existing inventory has not yet been cleared, and new batches continue to arrive, so the owners are extremely willing to sell early, so without large-scale sales, prices are unlikely to rise. The market originally looked small yesterday, but because the local market was active and the Fujian market continued to see sales, it was able to stabilize. The Tong Market handled 584 bags of Jiangxi machine-milled late rice at 8 yuan, 9 jiao to 8 yuan, 8 jiao and a half, 1,000 bags of Hunan machine-milled oil rice at 9 yuan, 2 jiao and a half to 8 yuan, 9 jiao and 2 fen, Quanzhou handled 100 bags of Hunan machine-milled Yuan rice at 10 yuan, 6 jiao, Fuzhou handled 340 bags of Wu machine-milled Yuan rice at 10 yuan, 6 jiao and a half, and 300 bags of Xiang machine-milled red rice at 8 yuan, 6 jiao. Prices were similar to yesterday.

Very Little Improvement in the Miscellaneous Grains Market 184

▲Even Less Vitality in the Oil Market

(Miscellaneous Grains) Yesterday, all markets trended downwards. The green bean market was large, with the dish green beans appearing flat but secretly loose. The remaining types such as bright green beans and hairy green beans had already fallen more than before. Because owners are still trying hard to sell, and buyers adhere to the principle of only buying if it's cheap, the market was unable to stabilize. Yellow beans also continued to be revised downwards, and sales remained sluggish, but the source did not stop, and the market remained silent. The sesame market was also weak, but red sorghum remained stable, and corn was also steady. The owner of raw red high-quality goods tried to sell, but because the sales area market was weak, they also adopted a wait-and-see attitude, so there were no transactions. (Oil Market (Soybean Oil)) Because the production area reported small quantities, the receiver was helpless, so there was no market for two days. According to industry insiders, the oil market needs to shed 1 or 2 qian to attract buyers. Yesterday, 900 dan of Tongzhou Mao Zhuang oil was traded at 10 taels and 8 qian, with delivery in Shen in February and March, handled by a wooden street business.

Flour Market Still Flat and Weak 185

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, each month showed a trend of initial stability followed by weakness. The quoted price of foreign wheat fell slightly, but the market's sentiment was raised by the previous day's actions by 客帮(travelling merchants) (from Andong and Tianjin). People inevitably thought that sales would become active and prices would improve. Therefore, when opening prices, sentiment was strong, and near and far terms were 7 li and a half to 1 fen and a half better than the previous day. However, by the second session, sales by 客帮(travelling merchants) did not move, and 津帮(Tianjin merchants) also continued to watch, so buying interest was silent. At that time, some small factories slightly reduced their offerings in the near and far terms, causing the market to fall again. At present, formal 客帮(travelling merchants) have not yet started, but the production of factories can increase due to the import of foreign wheat. From now on, the key will depend on how supply and demand play out. As a result, this month's prices were actually 2 li and a half lower than the previous day, February's prices remained unchanged, April's prices were 5 li higher, May's prices were 5 li lower, June's prices remained unchanged, and July's prices were 5 li lower.

Rotating Wheat Futures 186

Yesterday morning the wheat market initially appeared stable, followed by fatigue. The opening, price of foreign wheat saw a small increase and the short, outside of the market, still were buying positions, with the months of February and March rising an additional 2 fen. Because, there was no one to maintain positions this trend reversed towards fatigue. The remaining months remained equal to one another. By the time the market opened for trade there was an inflexibility in the flour market, sentiment began to shake, and the quoted price for each month softened slightly. The factories in Hankou and Zhenjiang were heard to have established a purchase of Australian Wheat at a price of 3 Liang 5 qian and 7.5 fen. With that, prospects for improvements in the wheat market became difficult. As a result, this month was better than the day prior by 1 fen and the months of March and April were down 1 fen.

Business Sutras (III)

Honey Dates and Apple Jujubes 190

Honey dates are produced in Anhui, Lanxi, Jiaxing, and other places. The Anhui goods are the best, followed by Lanxi goods, and then Jiaxing goods. When making dates, white core dates are used as the base. The surface of the date is cut into many lines with a knife to allow the sugar juice to penetrate easily. The knife work of Anhui dates is the most exquisite. South goods stores have the title of gold thread amber honey dates in their market advertisements, which describes the fineness of the knife lines and the bright color of the dates, hence they are listed as the top grade. Moreover, their date base is also good, with thick flesh and small pits, which is their characteristic. The grade of honey dates is distinguished by the size of the date. Those that are neither too big nor too small are called tutus. Tuts are used as the standard when opening prices. For each grade above tutus, 5 qian is added. For each grade below, 1 liang is deducted. The names of the goods are listed below: "Huan Ding", "Ding Ding", "Ding Mian", "Da Mian", "Mian Mian", "Tu Mian", "Tu Tu", "Gong Mian", "Quan Mian", "Shang Shang", "Zheng Kui", "Fu Kui". For example, if the opening price of Anhui tutus is 20 liang, the above will be added accordingly. Then tu mian will be 20.5 liang, mian mian will be 21 liang. The below will be reduced accordingly. Then gong mian will be 19 liang, and quan mian will be 18 liang. And so on. However, in case of shortage of goods or excessive cheapness, the price will vary slightly. In addition, Fujian and Tianjin also have products, but not in large quantities, so they are omitted here.

There are also those made with the method of apple honey dates, called apple dates. They are large in size, good in color, and have a special taste.

Honey dates and euryale ferox and lotus seeds are boiled into soup, which is bitter, fragrant, and delicious. Other ingredients, such as mung beans and pastries, also use honey dates to decorate them.

Free Talk

The Strange Coachman (by G.K. Chesterton, translated by) 216

— Shi Heng

The day I met the strange coachman was when I and three or four of my best friends were having a small meal at a small hotel in Sowerby. My best friends were either elusive skeptics or completely helpless believers, so our debates over drinks turned to the ultimate, terrifying thoughts. And the whole debate was entangled, finally thinking this: that is, the question is whether a person can fundamentally be certain of something? I think a person can be certain of something (as I told my friends, I roared and brandished an empty bottle), because if a person cannot rationally recognize a certainty, then what is this unrecognized certainty? If I have never experienced something like certainty, I cannot even say that something is uncertain. Similarly, if I have never experienced something like green, I cannot say that my nose is not green. If I really haven't seen green, maybe it is extremely green. So we shouted at each other, shaking the room; because metaphysics is a thoroughly emotional game, and the differences of opinion between us were very deep, as when talking about such things as so-called magnanimity or the development of intelligence. Because my friend had said that he unfolds his intelligence, as the sun unfolds the leaves of a palm tree, opening for the sake of opening, infinitely and eternally. But I said that I unfold my intelligence, as I open my mouth, to close on something certain and then close again. Just then my mouth was doing this work. And I enthusiastically pointed out, what a big fool I would be if I opened my mouth infinitely and eternally?

×××××

So when this debate ended, or at least when it was cut off (because it will never end), I came out with one of my companions, who somehow became a Member of Parliament in the chaos and considerable arrogance of the general election. So I sat with him in a carriage, running from the square of Leicester to the door of the House of Commons, where the police greeted me with special attention. Whether the police thought he was my protector, or I was his protector, this debate continues between us to this day.

In this narrative, maintaining the extreme detail of the facts is necessary. After my friend left the parliament, I hired a carriage to an office on Victoria Street, which I needed to visit, about several hundred yards away. So I jumped out of the carriage and gave him extra fare. He looked at the money, but not in the way that ordinary coachmen do, making people suspect that he was intentionally trying to rob. But this one was not an ordinary, perhaps not even a human, coachman. Revealing a foolish, childlike, and clearly very genuine surprise, he looked at the money: "You see, sir," he said, "you only gave me one shilling and eight pence." I replied to him with slight surprise, that I myself was very clear about. "But you know, sir," he said gently, pleadingly, hopefully, "that's not enough to pay for the carriage from Euston." "Euston," I repeated vaguely, because at the time this place name sounded to me like China and Arabia. "What exactly does Euston have to do with us?" "You were hailing me outside Euston Station," the man said with surprising accuracy, "and you said—" "What the devil are you talking about?" I said with gentlemanly tolerance. "I hired you from the west corner of Leicester Square." "Leicester!" he cried, revealing an extraordinary contempt, "We haven't been anywhere near Leicester Square today. You were hailing me outside Euston Station, and you said—" "Are you crazy, or am I crazy?" I asked him with scientific calmness. (To be continued)

Immortal 217

— Peng Jiahuang

It is rumored that cultivators can become immortals if they do not eat for three to five years. When I was a child, I also heard stories of cultivators who did not eat, saying that the cultivators sat cross-legged in a wooden cage by the roadside year after year. The wooden cage only had a small round hole for people to donate incense money. No one could get in or out of the small hole. Children and curious people often went to peek and always saw the cultivators not eating, living there. Although the cultivators disappeared later as people forgot about them, it was absolutely true that not eating could make one an immortal.

As far as I know, Westerners don’t eat much rice either, but they like to eat things like bread, beef, and eggs. Northerners in our country don’t eat much rice either, but they have to eat big noodles, corn buns, steamed buns, and boiled dumplings. If they don’t have these things to eat, they eat tree bark and yellow soil. Only after there is no more tree bark and yellow soil to eat, are they willing to become immortals.

I heard that in modern Western Europe, a kind of person has been invented who does not eat rice or become an immortal, and can also do what ordinary people do, but needs to eat a little electricity.

As for China, not wanting Western Europe to monopolize this, in recent years, a kind of person has also been invented who is unwilling to become an immortal and does not like to eat tree bark and yellow soil. They want to eat rice, but they have no rice to eat. They gather in groups, surge from here to there, riot and cause trouble, always making those who have rice to eat unhappy and restless. In the end, people feed them "deportation," and then that place is peaceful!

What to do when they arrive in another place? Naturally, they are still fed "deportation." Finally, they are fed "deportation to the world." After going around many circles, they finally become immortals!

All living beings, from the moment they are born, should see through the mortal world and cultivate to become immortals. Only then will this world be peaceful. This world is the heaven that we, who want to eat rice but have no rice to eat, dream of day and night.

"God, merciful Lord, please open the gates of heaven!"

Women Moving Forward 218

— Jian Feng

In the past, people always thought that women were only good for being men's toys, and there was no other use besides that. Even Auguste Comte, the founder of sociology, said that men should support women. In other words, women have no ability to be economically independent. However, in recent years, the contributions of Madame Curie in France to chemistry, the authority of Mrs. Yarov in finance and journalism, the activities of Madame Kollontai in Russia in the diplomatic world, and the glorious new records recently created by Ms. Amy Johnson in the British aviation world – these facts have shattered the previous erroneous views of belittling women. As long as women are willing to work hard, it can be said that they have almost the same ability as men, whether in academic aspects or in general work aspects.

Before the October Revolution, Russian women were also in an oppressed position like women in other countries around the world. However, after the success of the revolution, their status suddenly increased, which is absolutely beyond the reach of women in other European and American countries. Women in England, America, France, Germany, Spain, and Sweden have undergone countless difficult struggles for the movement for women's suffrage and the right to be elected, but the freedom and equality they demanded have not been fully obtained. Although Russian women were not as enthusiastic as women in the United States in the past for the movement for the right to participate in politics, they instead gained practical equal opportunities to participate in politics. At the time of the outbreak of the October Revolution in 1917, it was declared that equality should be given to the general public; therefore, the distinction between genders was abolished, and everyone, men and women, shared the work together. As a result, women were fairly distributed in all aspects, and it can be said that they were almost in the same position as men.

Lenin once said that as long as women, who account for half of the national population, are still bound in the kitchen, no matter what, the nation cannot be said to have completely gained freedom. Therefore, the handling of housework by Russian women after the transformation is exactly the opposite of that of French women: in today's Russia, public kitchens are set up for eating, and cooks who are good at cooking are hired to handle the work; public laundries are set up for washing, using the latest washing machines, and employing specialized workers. Mothers hand over their babies to nannies in nurseries to raise after giving birth, and they do not have to work hard day and night. In this way, women in general have extra time to seek knowledge and can actively participate in work to promote social progress. In Russia, family life does not hinder women's careers. Women now have equal opportunities, and men and women receive the same wages for doing the same work. Men and women each choose the occupation that best suits them, so women do not have to rely on their husbands' economic support. Of course, due to physiological reasons, there are many jobs that are too heavy for women to do.

Secondly, let us observe in terms of political administration. Women participate in all positions: they all have the practical ability to handle affairs. Women account for 8% of the main ruling bodies in Russia. Ms. Kollontai's skills in diplomatic activities and her reputation are known to the world; there are many women in Russia like her who have talents. According to a 1926 survey, there were 146 female judges and 20 female prosecutors in Russia, and the number has increased significantly in recent years. From the electrical industry to various industries, women participate in them, and the front line of women's occupations is expanding day by day.

In terms of education, male and female students in all universities enjoy equal rights, and it seems that they will surpass the universities in other European and American countries, which is envious of university students in other European and American countries. Russian women certainly do not hope that a few women will occupy high positions or show off. Their highest goal is to promote the development of the entire society; what they are doing day and night is for this purpose. Gorky once said that Russia is not aimed at material completion as the ultimate goal; in addition, it must build a sound spiritual culture. Russian women are now working together with men to bravely move forward on this road, in order to carry out their ideals.

A Trip to Luojia Mountain (2) 219

— Ms. Wen Juan

The round-domed buildings on the east side, the more exquisitely built ones, are the sites of the science and engineering colleges. Many experimental equipment are displayed in the circular auditorium. The library and classrooms are also much wider than those of the liberal arts college. We saw this place in a cursory manner, and we couldn't help but feel admiration for the appearance of the university. However, this solemn appearance can't match the magic power of the gentle autumn waves of East Lake, which makes us have to abandon Wuhan University and run to the side of East Lake; the water in the lake is really lovely, calm and clear. The autumn sky does not have her elegance, and the beautiful eyes of a beauty do not have her affection. She has an evergreen youth, a pure and flawless heart. The misty twilight covers her with a layer of soft veil, and the slender shadows of the sails paint her a pure white and delicate soul. At this time, it is exactly the time when the evening glow shines on the water and the twilight is vast. Her color slightly shows some blurred red halo and light green phantom. The white smoke pushes the sky light on the edge of the water gradually farther and farther, and the glory of the setting sun replaces the previous scene, applying a touch of rouge to the lake waves. Therefore, the twilight smoke is woven into the shadows of the clouds, and the white seagulls are woven into the peaceful sky, making it impossible to distinguish the boundary between water and sky, red-purple and light green. However, all this dyeing and all this transfiguration are all for the sake of this lake's heart. The smile disappears as soon as it appears, and it loses its own face, disappearing to the land of nothingness. This clear virgin heart still restores her original purity without being affected in the slightest.

Looking west, the setting sun has changed from deep yellow to crimson. This completely round sun stands proudly in the vast space. Above her is the bright blue sky, without a cloud blocking her way, and below her is a ring of bluish-green mist, waiting for the shining of her glory, which can create her pink future. However, a thin fence has been built around this beautiful fireball, as if unwilling to share the light with others! The faint trace of Hongshan below and the vast twilight hold up this crimson setting sun together, standing faintly on the western horizon. The mysterious light, the subtle color... "Even if Froebel were resurrected, I am afraid he would not be able to use the most appropriate and only words to describe even one ten-thousandth of it," C said, sighing slightly.

The young N and H seemed a little bored that we were so fascinated by the scenery. They said, "It's very close to Zhuodao Spring here. Why don't we go play for a while? Let's go now, there's still time."

I also agreed happily. But after setting off, my heart felt hesitant again, but after all, I had already gone halfway, and it was impossible not to go.

I broke off a few wild camellias along the way. The white petals still retained the past beauty. I carefully inserted them into the lapel of my clothes. Passing through several pine forests, it was a pity that there was no wind that day, so I could not hear the secluded rhyme of the pine waves. But I saw the lush green shade all over the ground. The ancient trees towered into the sky. This is the most densely forested place in Luojia Mountain.

"This area is very good, but it's a bit too gloomy. It's a bit like a small poem by Hardy, where beauty and sadness are mixed together," C said quietly. He is good at foreign literature, so foreign writers' names always come out of his mouth as soon as he opens it.

While we were talking, N and H had already jumped over the stone archway, running and jumping. (To be continued)

Talks

Clearly Recognize the Way Out and the Dead End! 221

The way out is the bright path to seek survival from death, the dead end is to run wildly at will, regardless of gains and losses, and go straight into the dark tunnel of hell. Between heaven and earth, these two roads are parallel and side by side everywhere. People in the world do not observe carefully, and move forward blindly. If they are lucky, they will reach the paradise, and if they are unlucky, they will fall into hell. The two roads are dangerous, and it is necessary to recognize them as soon as possible.

Reviewing the past and verifying the present, whether it is the personal life and career, or the rise and fall and survival of a country and nation in both hemispheres, whenever a problem is at hand, the prerequisite is to immediately distinguish the way out from the dead end? With the prerequisite conditions, there is hope for the result of victory; otherwise, if the eyebrows are on fire, and you only care about the present, and blindly follow the muddleheaded way, not only will the result of victory not be achieved in the future, but even the hope of survival will not be grasped.

Readers, please do not doubt that my words are close to being arbitrary. May I ask Yuan Shikai in the early years of the Republic of China: If he did not take the dead end of a family world? Not only would he not be notorious for thousands of years, but he would also be famous in the history books, comparable to Washington of the United States. It is also a pity for those suicidal compatriots who take their lives lightly in recent times. The reason why they take their lives lightly is that they are all aware of themselves and have entered a fork in the road that cannot be recovered. However, if an individual goes astray, they can still seek other interests and do not have to die. If a certain country and nation makes a mistake in policy and doctrine, resulting in entering a fork in the road and a dead end, that is destined to be a disaster for the country. For example, pre-war Germany, if it did not dream of military aggression, how could it have declined to the present level? Based on these precedents, I can prove that the remnants of the former Qing Dynasty丨Puyi丨Zheng Xiaoxu, etc., are heading into the dark tunnel of hell, and Japan is also eager to taste the spicy taste of Germany after the European war.

Now our national crisis is urgent, as dangerous as stacked eggs. Which way can we go? I have clearly recognized "Out of the Pass"! Furthermore, with 120,000 points of sincerity, I advise the compatriots who are preparing to commit suicide not to make meaningless sacrifices, the corrupt and inferior local tyrants not to specialize in their own pockets, the old and new warlords not to blindly fight privately, the green forest bandits and communists not to arbitrarily make trouble, the important party and national figures not to each have their own opinions, and the senior military officers not to be timid and cowardly. Everyone should hold on to the doctrine of "rather be a shattered jade than a complete tile" 丨immediately mobilize, whether it is a big gun, a small gun, a Green Dragon Crescent Blade, or a knife for slaughtering chickens and cows, gather them all together and kill them out of the pass together丨丨Fight to the death with the enemy丨In the future, even if we are unfortunate and die in the natural large refrigerator-like place outside the pass? I believe that our bones can be preserved for a longer time without decay 丨We swear not to stop until we achieve the goal of restoring our lost territories丨This method is the only broad and correct way for the Chinese nation to seek survival.

Otherwise, if we still cling to the biased view of "first secure the interior, then resist foreign aggression"? I dare say that the interior will not be secured, and the country will perish first.

Way out! Dead end丨Paradise! Hell丨Compatriots, recognize clearly.

Science

More Misnamed Products 223

— Railway Sleepers

(V) Bakelite

Bakelite is named so because it's a non-conductive material often used in electrical appliances. It's also named so because of its tough texture, lightness, and ease of carving, resembling wood. In reality, it's a product of the chemical industry. Its main raw material is carbonic acid, supplemented by rosin, sulfur, sulfuric acid, carbolic acid, etc. It can be made into various patterns and colors. Its properties, besides being non-conductive and tough, include being shatterproof and unbreakable. However, it is extremely vulnerable to fire, which is its only weakness and cause of destruction. Its uses are widespread: accessories for electrical appliances, fountain pen barrels, other decorations, daily utensils, etc., all require bakelite.

(VI) Refined Steel

On the market, there are silver-gray, shiny metal daily utensils, such as woks and spatulas for gas stoves, as well as rice cookers, rice bowls, and mirror frames. These are all made of this material, commonly called "refined steel." But what is it really? It's not steel at all, let alone "refined." It's cast from another metal – aluminum. Aluminum has a specific gravity of 2.7, making it one of the lightest metals. It's ductile and can be pressed into extremely thin sheets, and its melting point is high, above 650 degrees Celsius. This is why it's chosen for manufacturing daily furniture. Furthermore, it has a protective layer of aluminum oxide (Al2O3) covering the surface. This layer of aluminum oxide prevents the aluminum underneath from being oxidized or corroded by air, while the exterior forms a shiny, silver-gray appearance, making it both aesthetically pleasing and durable, truly a great achievement of science. However, be careful when using it not to cook foods with excessive salt content. Salt easily dissolves in water, and in large quantities, it undergoes chemical reactions to produce caustic soda, hydrochloric acid, caustic magnesia, etc., all of which are strong substances that can corrode the aluminum oxide and even the aluminum underneath. Because the "refined steel" utensils are often made of extremely thin aluminum foil, people often find their rice cookers, woks, etc., corroded and leaking. This is a drawback of "refined steel."

(VII) Chalk

Chalk, also known as whiting, is indispensable in schools. Its chemical name is calcium carbonate, a compound of lime suspension and carbonic acid. Although it's a very simple chemical reaction, the scale of manufacturing is not small due to scientific conditions. Besides being used for writing on blackboards, chalk has a great water absorption capacity, so many students in schools use it to replace blotting paper. If you don't believe it, try it and you'll see it's true.

(VIII) Carborundum

Carborundum is a crystalline form of carbon related to diamond. Carborundum is a compound of carbon, but it is not a diamond. Its process involves using a resistance furnace, placing layers of sand and carbon chips between the two electrodes. When current passes through, the resistance generates enormous high-temperature heat, causing the sand (silicon dioxide) and carbon to combine and form this carborundum. Its formula is SiC. It is an extremely hard material. The small particles used by ordinary shops to cut glass are made of this carborundum material. Its powder, when mixed with other viscous substances, can be placed in molds to create grinding stones essential in metalworking factories. Therefore, this is an extremely useful product. It also has an advantage: unlike diamonds, which melt when exposed to fire, it is a product of furnaces and is not afraid of small fires. You can place it anywhere without worrying about it!

Jottings from the Quiet Studio 224

— Flood

Gongs, drums, and firecrackers sound all day long, and people are celebrating the happy New Year with beaming faces. Alas! They have probably forgotten the bloody battle of Shanghai last year, the brave fighting and flesh flying of our loyal soldiers, and the displacement and devastation of the people in the war zone! Otherwise, how could they be so happy?

According to recent news reports, Japan continues to increase its troops near the Yuguan Pass in Rehe, actively implementing its consistent continental policy, preparing to invade Jehol on a large scale. What are the gentlemen who are constantly shouting "Resist humiliation and save the country, long-term resistance" actually planning to do?

As usual, before the movie starts, there are many advertisements, either for winter supplements or the opening of X restaurant at discounted prices. Now, the first thing that comes into our view is a New Year's greeting advertisement: "Happy New Year... Do not forget national humiliation." Cinema boss! You really can't stand this China with its internal troubles and external threats, so you have to put a few striking words on the screen to stimulate the audience to do something? No, I think it is because you are pursuing your so-called "entertainment does not forget to save the country, saving the country does not forget entertainment" with such painstaking effort! You smart boss! How can we not bow down to you!

Originally, Mrs. Cheng, who always takes a car, doesn't know why, but today she also advocates exercise and uses her honorable legs. This is at midnight. She pointed and said: "These prostitutes standing in the whistling north wind will not feel the pain of life. If they can feel it, why not use their omnipotent hands to work? So there is no need to pity them at all." So after hearing this, I was speechless.

The ×× lottery has already been drawn. Of course, everyone's mind is full of hope of winning the lottery, dreaming of gold. But now, the majority has turned from hope to disappointment. Friends! Please wake up and stop indulging in dreams of gold! The transformation of the times has gradually amplified its dazzling brilliance. Why not find the path you should take?

Correspondence from Store Employees

Bringing it on Oneself 225

Dear Editor:

I have a very difficult problem to solve, and I am telling you about it; please give me clear guidance. The thing is this: the house I live in is my own: because it is too big, I have called in a few tenants. One of them is surnamed Wang, and she is a distant relative of ours. There are only two of them, a mother and daughter; the mother is about forty years old, and the daughter is only seventeen years old; their male master has been dead for a long time. They have lived in our house for many years; before I came out to do business, I lived at home every day and kept this woman company, so the two sides actually developed love. In the year she was fifteen years old, I also had physical relations with her. At that time, the two sides were so affectionate and entangled, full of the idea of "lovers eventually becoming dependents." Now I have a business and have to leave her. Unexpectedly, she has completely changed her former character. All day long, she runs outside; and six or seven days out of ten, she even stays outside at night; looking at her behavior, it seems that she has another lover. I went back last time to advise her, but she still didn't listen; and I heard that it is even worse now. So I wrote a letter to her to break up with her; I didn't expect her reply to say, "I must marry you, and if you don't allow it, I will solve it legally, or I will commit suicide."

Dear Editor: I absolutely do not want to marry her, and my parents cannot agree to this marriage either. But after breaking up with her, if she sues me in court, will I be charged with the regulations of rape of an underage girl? Or if she does not sue in court and really commits suicide, then her mother will certainly report me. Then what is my sin? Please tell me clearly, and also teach me how to deal with myself. Finally, I have to state that I am nine years older than her. (End excerpt)

Respectfully, Chen Mengqiao

○○○

Editor's Note: After reading Mr. Chen's letter, we fully understand the pain in his heart at the moment. But after much research, we finally feel that we cannot find any reason to forgive him in law or morality. Let us describe in detail the observation points of his facts in law and morality: We hope that Mr. Chen can think calmly and bear the consequences of the evil causes he has sown. At the same time, we hope that young people who are on the wrong path will wake up quickly. Don't be impulsive for a while, and act willfully, causing yourself to eat your own fruits; then you will not betray the original intention of our publishing this communication.

(I) Legal observation: When Mr. Chen had physical relations with Ms. Wang, Ms. Wang was only fifteen years old, while Mr. Chen was already twenty-four years old. Therefore, although it was because it came from the other party's consent, it did not constitute the "aggravated rape crime" of "rape of a woman under the age of sixteen"; but it did constitute the "quasi-rape crime" of "consensual intercourse with a woman under the age of sixteen", which should be sentenced to imprisonment of seven years or more according to law. Fortunately, this is a private prosecution crime; unless Ms. Wang or her mother reports it, the law can forgive and not ask. Now, assuming that the marriage contract is cancelled (although there is no formal engagement, but the verbal expression of each other's meaning is also considered a marriage contract by law), no matter how Ms. Wang's infidelity can be proven; even if there is real evidence, it can only constitute the condition for canceling the marriage contract, and in no way can it be used to remove the responsibility of adultery. Therefore, once the other party is angered because of the termination of the contract, they will naturally report it immediately; at that time, Mr. Chen will have to prepare for at least seven years of prison life. In case the other party commits suicide out of anger, it will be even worse. Because the law has long prepared such a clause, saying that "those who commit rape and cause the victim to commit suicide out of shame and anger shall be sentenced to imprisonment of fifteen years or more." Waiting for your visit!

(II) Moral observation: Whether Ms. Wang has another lover, we believe that we cannot arbitrarily conclude that she is unfaithful just because she often spends the night outside. Judging from the fact that Ms. Wang insists on marrying Mr. Chen, we feel that Mr. Wang is inevitably paranoid. In short, without real evidence, it cannot be said. Even if we take a step back and say that Ms. Wang does have this kind of behavior; then this is also Mr. Chen's own fault. "At the beginning of man, his nature is good", the reason for Ms. Wang's bad habits is still planted when Mr. Chen first destroyed her virginity!

We also know very well that love cannot accommodate more than one person at the same time, so the spouse's exclusive thinking about the other party is considered to be correct. But before marriage, the other party's virginity seems to be more lenient. It is only necessary that after marriage, there is no third party involved. It is inevitable to insist on marrying a virgin as a wife. Based on the above reasons, Mr. Chen seems to be able to marry Ms. Wang. If after marriage, it is found that she still has relationships with other lovers intermittently, it may not be impossible to file for divorce again.

Novel

A Family of Scholars and Officials (Continued from XI) 227

— Wang Zhongxian

(6) The conscience was eaten by a demon star

In the vast sea from the South China Sea to Shanghai, a large 5,000-ton merchant ship, fully loaded with passengers and foreign goods, broke through the deep blue sea water and moved forward at full speed. The ship's sharp bow cut through the plane of the sea. On both sides of the bow, two snow-white waves surged up, as if they were always attached to the ship's forward movement. There was also a large group of white seagulls, clustering around the large ship, following day and night, as if they were afraid that the passengers would be lonely on the long journey, and deliberately followed to be good companions at sea. The passengers trapped in the cabin, in this vast and boundless environment, felt more and more the insignificance of human life. If they left this ship, they would immediately become Robinson Crusoe, who would be 90% dead. When they looked at this group of seagulls, sometimes soaring in the sky and sometimes floating in the heart of the waves, they would all have the fantasy that "I am not as good as them."

At that time, it was dusk, the sun had already disappeared below the horizon, and the eastern sky was as dark as paint. Only where the sun had set was there still a piece of yellow light, reflected on the sea surface, which could also be transformed into several golden snakes, wriggling and dancing. The passengers watching the sunset on the deck also went down to the cabin one after another. Only on a rattan couch in the recessed area behind the driving bridge was there still a fashionable woman lying, with her beautiful hair blown into a messy fluff. A handsome young man was sitting on the armrest of the rattan chair. He used his body to block her face, afraid that the sea breeze would blow her badly. People on the ship saw them whispering to each other, very affectionately, and they all said that they were a newlywed couple, enjoying the happy life of a honeymoon trip. Who knew that they were actually close relatives, an uncle and sister-in-law!

With the conscience of heaven and earth, Xia Youzhong never dreamed that he would betray his conscience and invade his brother's lover. However, Ai Ruohua had been planning this for a long time. She had always taken care of Youzhong meticulously. Youzhong thought she was especially virtuous as a sister-in-law, and would never have any improper thoughts. Who knew that when she got on the ship, she completely showed her attitude. When Youzhong was very worried and discussing with her how to rescue Zhongnan, she said indifferently:

"This is his own fault, he can't live!"

Youzhong was surprised and said, "He is your husband, how can you say such a thing?"

Ruohua said lazily: "It doesn't matter if you have this kind of evil and savage husband or not! As long as you are not involved, I don't care about anyone else." After she finished speaking, she squinted at him with her pretty eyes, followed by a charming smile, full of charm, which scared Youzhong and he didn't dare to open his mouth for a long time. Her love fire was burning and could no longer be contained, so she completely told him her secret love for him. Youzhong said with a guilty conscience:

"It's not that I don't love you, I just don't dare to have such bad thoughts, because I am still young, and I will do some business in society in the future. If I fall in love with you, it will be a disreputable thing. If my brother knows, it will be terrible. Even if I hide it from him, if outsiders know, my personality will be swept away! How will I be able to stand in society in the future?"

Ruohua pointed at his forehead with her slender finger, and then smiled: "You are really a child, people can't help but say that you are a fool! In this era, as long as you have money, where can't you eat? The missionaries who preach Jesus's doctrines have the most personality, earning only twenty dollars a month! The profiteers who sell enemy goods, the warlords who kill and set fires, the hooligans who protect opium, the politicians who are two-faced, and the corrupt officials who scrape the ground for money, as well as all kinds of shameless things, they are all people with no personality, but they have money in their pockets and are welcomed everywhere, who dares to say half a sentence about them? Now it is a world where gold is omnipotent, if you lose your personality, as long as you have gold, you can buy it back. If you have no money, you cannot be a human being, and if you have no personality, you can still be a high official and make a fortune. Have you seen anyone who has been looked down upon because they have lost their personality? Besides, free love is a legitimate thing, how many of the first-class rich people and the first-class fashionable ladies have been married through three matchmakers and six certificates?"

Youzhong was rebutted by her, speechless, staring at her foolishly, without any expression. Ruohua held him down and asked:

"Little one, have you made up your mind?"
